- Second term: `5.6497*epsilon*(T² - 685.157*T + 117,399.97)`

  = `5.6497*epsilon*T² - 3871.0*epsilon*T + 663,268*epsilon`

= `5.6497*epsilon*T² - 3872.18*epsilon*T + 663,696*epsilon`

So GT = **epsilon * (A*T² + B*T + C)** where A, B, C are specific constants.

This is a polynomial in epsilon and T: `epsilon*T²`, `epsilon*T`, and `epsilon` terms only.

Key structural requirement: GT is **linear in epsilon** and **quadratic in T**, with no constant term (everything multiplied by epsilon).

Now I'll check candidates for structural match:

**Candidate 4:** `c0*sin(...) + c3*epsilon³ + c4*epsilon² + c5*epsilon*(T+c6)^c7 + c8*epsilon`

If we set c0=0 (kill sin), c3=0 (kill ε³), c4=0 (kill ε²), and set c7=2:
= `c5*epsilon*(T+c6)² + c8*epsilon`
= `c5*epsilon*(T² + 2*c6*T + c6²) + c8*epsilon`
= `c5*epsilon*T² + 2*c5*c6*epsilon*T + (c5*c6² + c8)*epsilon`

This matches the GT structure! We need:
- c5 = 5.6497
- c6 = -342.578 (so c5*c6 matches the T coefficient)
- 2*c5*c6 = -3872.18 → 2*5.6497*(-342.578) = -3872.18 ✓
- c5*c6² + c8 = 663,696

Let me verify: c5*c6² = 5.6497*(342.578)² = 5.6497*117,400 ≈ 663,268. Then c8 ≈ 427.58.

And from GT: the linear epsilon coefficient is 427.58 + 663,268 = 663,696. So c8 = 663,696 - 663,268 = 428. Close enough (rounding).

**Candidate 4 matches!**

Let me also verify **Candidate 58:** `T*c0*(c1+epsilon)² + c2*sin(...) + c5*epsilon*(T+c6)^c7 + c8*epsilon`

Setting c2=0 (kill sin), c7=0 (making (T+c6)^0 = 1):

= `c5*epsilon*(T+c6)² + c8*epsilon` which works same as Candidate 4.
